<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>EX-99.1</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Microsoft Store announces new approach to retail </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Microsoft to continue to support customers online, with retail team members working remotely and at Microsoft corporate locations </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>REDMOND, Wash. &#151; June</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;26, 2020 &#151;</B><B></B> <U>Microsoft Corp.</U> (NASDAQ:
MSFT)&nbsp;(&#147;Microsoft&#148;)&nbsp;today announced a strategic change in its retail operations, including closing Microsoft Store physical locations. The company&#146;s retail team members will continue to serve customers from Microsoft
corporate facilities and remotely providing sales, training, and support. Microsoft will continue to invest in its digital storefronts on Microsoft.com, and stores in Xbox and Windows,&nbsp;reaching more than 1.2&nbsp;billion people every&nbsp;month
in 190 markets. The company will also reimagine spaces that serve&nbsp;all customers, including operating Microsoft Experience Centers in London, NYC, Sydney, and Redmond campus locations. The closing of Microsoft Store physical locations will
result in a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> charge of approximately $450M, or $0.05 per share, to be recorded in the current quarter ending June&nbsp;30, 2020. The charge includes primarily asset write-offs and impairments. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;Our sales have grown online as our product portfolio has evolved to largely digital offerings, and our talented team has proven success serving
customers beyond any physical location,&#148; said Microsoft Corporate Vice President David Porter. &#147;We are grateful to our Microsoft Store customers and we look forward to continuing to serve them online and with our retail sales team at
Microsoft corporate locations.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Since the Microsoft Store locations closed in late March due to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic, the retail team has helped small businesses and education customers digitally transform; virtually trained hundreds of thousands of enterprise and education customers on remote work and
learning software; and helped customers with support calls. The team supported communities by hosting more than 14,000 online workshops and summer camps and more than 3,000 virtual graduations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;We deliberately built teams with unique backgrounds and skills that could serve customers from anywhere. The evolution of our workforce ensured we
could continue to serve customers of all sizes when they needed us most, working remotely these last months,&#148; said Porter. &#147;Speaking over 120 languages, their diversity reflects the many communities we serve. Our commitment to growing and
developing careers from this talent pool is stronger than ever.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">The retail team members will serve consumers, small-business, education, and
enterprise customers, while building a pipeline of talent with transferable skills. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;The Microsoft Store team has long been celebrated at
Microsoft and embodies our culture,&#148; said Microsoft Chief People Officer Kathleen Hogan. &#147;The team has a proven track record of attracting, motivating, and developing diverse talent. This infusion of talent is invaluable for Microsoft and
creates opportunities for thousands of people.&#148;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">With significant growth through its digital storefronts, including Microsoft.com, and stores on
Xbox and Windows, the company will continue to invest in digital innovation across software and hardware. New services include 1:1 video chat support, online tutorial videos, and virtual workshops with more digital solutions to come. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;It is a new day for how Microsoft Store team members will serve all customers,&#148; said
Porter. &#147;We are energized about the opportunity to innovate in how we engage with all customers, maximize our talent for greatest impact, and most importantly help our valued customers achieve more.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>About Microsoft </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft (Nasdaq &#147;MSFT&#148;
@microsoft) enables digital transformation for the era of an intelligent cloud and an intelligent edge. Its mission is to empower every person and every organization on the planet to achieve more. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Forward-Looking Statements </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Statements in this release that
are &#147;forward-looking statements&#148; are based on current expectations and assumptions that are subject to risks and uncertainties. Actual results could differ materially because of factors such as: </P>
